## Instruction

```python
# Organize data by date, then by ticker
data_by_date = {}

for entry in aapl_data:
    date_str = datetime.fromisoformat(entry['Date'].replace('Z', '+00:00')).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    if date_str not in data_by_date:
        data_by_date[date_str] = {}
    data_by_date[date_str]['AAPL'] = entry

for entry in tsla_data:
    date_str = datetime.fromisoformat(entry['Date'].replace('Z', '+00:00')).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    if date_str not in data_by_date:
        data_by_date[date_str] = {}
    data_by_date[date_str]['TSLA'] = entry

# Sort dates
sorted_dates = sorted(data_by_date.keys())

print(f"Total trading days: {len(sorted_dates)}")
print(f"Date range: {sorted_dates[0]} to {sorted_dates[-1]}")
```

```python
aapl_data = json.loads(aapl_raw)

# Create organized data structure
data_by_date = {}
for entry in aapl_data:
    date_str = datetime.fromisoformat(entry['Date'].replace('Z', '+00:00')).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    if date_str not in data_by_date:
        data_by_date[date_str] = {}
    data_by_date[date_str]['AAPL'] = entry

# Get sorted dates
sorted_dates = sorted(data_by_date.keys())
print(f"Total dates: {len(sorted_dates)}")
print(f"First 5 dates: {sorted_dates[:5]}")
print(f"Sample data structure created successfully")
```

```python
import json

# I'll build the sheet data row by row
# Header row
sheet_data = [["Ticker", "Date", "Open", "High", "Low", "Close", "Volume"]]

# Sample dates and tickers
dates = ["2025-06-02", "2025-06-03"]
tickers = ["AAPL", "META", "NVDA", "TSLA"]

# Add sample rows
for date in dates:
    for ticker in tickers:
        sheet_data.append([ticker, date, "xx", "xx", "xx", "xx", "xx"])

print(f"Created {len(sheet_data)} rows (including header)")
print("First 10 rows:")
for i, row in enumerate(sheet_data[:10]):
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}")
 code
```

```python

import json

# Create a smaller script that will be saved to file
script_content = '''import json

# Stock data
stock_data = {}

# Read from the raw data file and parse it
# For now, let's create the structure directly

# Get all unique dates - we know we have 41 trading days
dates = [
    "2025-06-02", "2025-06-03", "2025-06-04", "2025-06-05", "2025-06-06",
    "2025-06-09", "2025-06-10", "2025-06-11", "2025-06-12", "2025-06-13",
    "2025-06-16", "2025-06-17", "2025-06-18", "2025-06-20", "2025-06-23",
    "2025-06-24", "2025-06-25", "2025-06-26", "2025-06-27", "2025-06-30",
    "2025-07-01", "2025-07-02", "2025-07-03", "2025-07-07", "2025-07-08",
    "2025-07-09", "2025-07-10", "2025-07-11", "2025-07-14", "2025-07-15",
    "2025-07-16", "2025-07-17", "2025-07-18", "2025-07-21", "2025-07-22",
    "2025-07-23", "2025-07-24", "2025-07-25", "2025-07-28", "2025-07-29",
    "2025-07-30"
]

print(f"Total trading days: {len(dates)}")
print(f"Date range: {dates[0]} to {dates[-1]}")
'''

# Save script
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/create_sheet_data.py', 'w') as f:
    f.write(script_content)

print("Script saved successfully")
```

```python
sheet_data = [["Ticker", "Date", "Open", "High", "Low", "Close", "Volume"]]

# Dates
dates = ["2025-06-02", "2025-06-03", "2025-06-04", "2025-06-05", "2025-06-06", "2025-06-09", "2025-06-10", "2025-06-11", "2025-06-12", "2025-06-13", "2025-06-16", "2025-06-17", "2025-06-18", "2025-06-20", "2025-06-23", "2025-06-24", "2025-06-25", "2025-06-26", "2025-06-27", "2025-06-30", "2025-07-01", "2025-07-02", "2025-07-03", "2025-07-07", "2025-07-08", "2025-07-09", "2025-07-10", "2025-07-11", "2025-07-14", "2025-07-15", "2025-07-16", "2025-07-17", "2025-07-18", "2025-07-21", "2025-07-22", "2025-07-23", "2025-07-24", "2025-07-25", "2025-07-28", "2025-07-29", "2025-07-30"]

# AAPL data (Open, High, Low, Close, Volume)
aapl = [[200.28,202.13,200.12,201.70,35423300],[201.35,203.77,200.96,203.27,46381600],[202.91,206.24,202.10,202.82,43604000],[203.50,204.75,200.15,200.63,55126100],[203.00,205.70,202.05,203.92,46607700],[204.39,206.00,200.02,201.45,72862600],[200.60,204.35,200.57,202.67,54672600],[203.50,204.50,198.41,198.78,60989900],[199.08,199.68,197.36,199.20,43904600],[199.73,200.37,195.70,196.45,51447300],[197.30,198.69,196.56,198.42,43020700],[197.20,198.39,195.21,195.64,38856200],[195.94,197.57,195.07,196.58,45394700],[198.24,201.70,196.86,201.00,96813500],[201.63,202.30,198.96,201.50,55814300],[202.59,203.44,200.20,200.30,54064000],[201.45,203.67,200.62,201.56,39525700],[201.43,202.64,199.46,201.00,50799100],[201.89,203.22,200.00,201.08,73188600],[202.01,207.39,199.26,205.17,91912800],[206.67,210.19,206.14,207.82,78788900],[208.91,213.34,208.14,212.44,67941800],[212.15,214.65,211.81,213.55,34955800],[212.68,216.23,208.80,209.95,50229000],[210.10,211.43,208.45,210.01,42848900],[209.53,211.33,207.22,211.14,48749400],[210.51,213.48,210.03,212.41,44443600],[210.57,212.13,209.86,211.16,39765800],[209.93,210.91,207.54,208.62,38840100],[209.22,211.89,208.92,209.11,42296300],[210.30,212.40,208.64,210.16,47490500],[210.57,211.80,209.59,210.02,48068100],[210.87,211.79,209.70,211.18,48974600],[212.10,215.78,211.63,212.48,51377400],[213.14,214.95,212.23,214.40,46404100],[215.00,215.15,212.41,214.15,46989300],[213.90,215.69,213.53,213.76,46022600],[214.70,215.24,213.40,213.88,40268800],[214.03,214.85,213.06,214.05,37858000],[214.18,214.81,210.82,211.27,51411700],[211.90,212.39,207.72,209.05,45512500]]
```

```python

import json

# Load existing data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_part1.json', 'r') as f:
```

```python

import json

# Load the data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_final.json', 'r') as f:
    old_data = json.load(f)

# Reorganize: header + for each date (AAPL, META, NVDA, TSLA)
header = old_data[0]
aapl_rows = old_data[1:42]  # rows 1-41
meta_rows = old_data[42:83]  # rows 42-82
nvda_rows = old_data[83:124]  # rows 83-123
tsla_rows = old_data[124:165]  # rows 124-164

# Create new organized data
new_data = [header]

# For each of the 41 dates, add all 4 tickers
for i in range(41):
    new_data.append(aapl_rows[i])
    new_data.append(meta_rows[i])
    new_data.append(nvda_rows[i])
    new_data.append(tsla_rows[i])

print(f"Reorganized data: {len(new_data)} rows")
print(f"First 10 rows:")
for i in range(min(10, len(new_data))):
    print(f"  Row {i}: {new_data[i][:3]}")  # Show first 3 columns

# Save
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_organized.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(new_data, f)

print("\nSaved to sheet_data_organized.json")
 code
```

```python
import json

# Parse the JSON data
```

```python

import json
import sys

# Load the complete dataset
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_organized.json', 'r') as f:
    sheet_data = json.load(f)

# Print info
print(f"Loaded {len(sheet_data)} rows")
print(f"Columns: {len(sheet_data[0])}")
print(f"First row (header): {sheet_data[0]}")
print(f"Second row (first data): {sheet_data[1]}")
print(f"Last row: {sheet_data[-1]}")

# Write a marker file to indicate data is ready
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/data_ready.txt', 'w') as f:
    f.write("Data is ready for upload\n")
    f.write(f"Rows: {len(sheet_data)}\n")
    f.write(f"Spreadsheet ID: 1rBj8_uQXCW-Fgezp_N3s-3if8Ko19N_9qWdYi9_sAso\n")
    f.write(f"Sheet: Jun-Jul_2025\n")
    f.write(f"Range: A1:G165\n")

print("\nData verification complete!")
 code
```

```python

import json

# Load the data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_organized.json', 'r') as f:
    full_data = json.load(f)

# For the API call, we need to format it properly
# Let's create a compact JSON string
data_json = json.dumps(full_data)

# Save to a file that can be used
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/upload_payload.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump({
        "spreadsheet_id": "1rBj8_uQXCW-Fgezp_N3s-3if8Ko19N_9qWdYi9_sAso",
        "sheet": "Jun-Jul_2025",
        "range": "A1:G165",
        "data": full_data
    }, f)

print("Upload payload created")
print(f"Data size: {len(data_json)} characters")
 code
```

```python

import json

# Read the organized data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_organized.json', 'r') as f:
    sheet_data = json.load(f)

# Prepare the data in the exact format needed
# Convert to ensure all types are JSON-serializable
formatted_data = []
for row in sheet_data:
    formatted_row = []
    for cell in row:
        formatted_row.append(cell)
    formatted_data.append(formatted_row)

# Save the formatted version
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/formatted_for_upload.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(formatted_data, f)

print(f"Formatted {len(formatted_data)} rows")
print("Ready for Google Sheets upload")

# Output the parameters we'll use
params = {
    "spreadsheet_id": "1rBj8_uQXCW-Fgezp_N3s-3if8Ko19N_9qWdYi9_sAso",
    "sheet": "Jun-Jul_2025",
    "range": "A1:G165"
}

print(f"\nParameters:")
for k, v in params.items():
    print(f"  {k}: {v}")
 code
```

```python

import json
import sys

# Load data from file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_data_organized.json', 'r') as f:
    upload_data = json.load(f)

# Verify it's correct
print(f"Data loaded: {len(upload_data)} rows")
print(f"First 3 rows:")
for i in range(min(3, len(upload_data))):
    print(f"  {upload_data[i]}")

# Now the data is in the variable upload_data
# We need to pass this to the Google Sheets API
# Let me save a reference
globals()['SHEET_DATA'] = upload_data
print("\nData stored in SHEET_DATA variable")
print(f"Type: {type(upload_data)}")
print(f"Ready for API call")
```

```python
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

# Create a function to process the data
def process_stock_data(data, ticker):
    df = pd.DataFrame(data)
    df['Ticker'] = ticker
    df['Date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['Date']).dt.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    return df[['Ticker', 'Date', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume']]
```

```python
        ["META", "2025-07-23", 706.37, 714.63, 704.93, 713.58, 8771600],
        ["META", "2025-07-24", 717.05, 723.62, 714.00, 714.80, 10920800],
        ["META", "2025-07-25", 716.92, 720.65, 711.90, 712.68, 8271700],
        ["META", "2025-07-28", 715.20, 724.74, 712.68, 717.63, 8715700],
        ["META", "2025-07-29", 720.00, 724.47, 699.91, 700.00, 13267000],
        ["META", "2025-07-30", 708.09, 708.50, 691.20, 695.21, 27077300]
    ]
    
    # Combine all data
    all_data = aapl_data + tsla_data + nvda_data + meta_data
    
    # Sort by date and ticker
    all_data.sort(key=lambda x: (x[1], x[0]))
    
    return all_data

# Get the data
stock_data = create_stock_data()

print(f"Total rows to add: {len(stock_data)}")
print("\nFirst 5 rows:")
for i, row in enumerate(stock_data[:5]):
    print(f"Row {i+1}: {row}")

print("\nLast 5 rows:")
for i, row in enumerate(stock_data[-5:]):
    print(f"Row {len(stock_data)-4+i}: {row}") code
```
